#GRAB CHALLENGER PLAYERS
URL = "https://na1.api.riotgames.com/lol/league/v4/challengerleagues/by-queue/RANKED_SOLO_5x5?api_key="+api_key
PARAMS = {'queue':'RANKED_SOLO_5x5', 'region':'na1'} 
api_key = 'REDACTED'
watcher = LolWatcher(api_key)
my_region = 'na1'

r = requests.get(url = URL, params = PARAMS) 
challengers = json.loads(json.dumps(r.json()))

In [3]:
#GRAB GRANDMASTER (GM) PLAYERS
gmURL = "https://na1.api.riotgames.com/lol/league/v4/grandmasterleagues/by-queue/RANKED_SOLO_5x5?api_key="+api_key
gmPARAMS = {'queue':'RANKED_SOLO_5x5', 'region':'na1'}
r = requests.get(url = gmURL, params = gmPARAMS)
gmRaw = json.loads(json.dumps(r.json()))
#gmRaw
In [4]:
#MAKE GM DATA FRAME
gmParticipants = []
for row in gmRaw['entries']:
    gmparticipants_row = {}
    gmparticipants_row['summonerId'] = row['summonerId']
    gmparticipants_row['summonerName'] = row['summonerName']
    gmparticipants_row['leaguePoints'] = row['leaguePoints']
    gmparticipants_row['wins'] = row['wins']
    gmparticipants_row['losses'] = row['losses']
    gmParticipants.append(gmparticipants_row)
gmPlayerTable = pd.DataFrame(gmParticipants)
gmPlayerTable['rank'] = 'Grandmaster'
gmPlayerTable

In [5]:
#MAKE CHALLENGER DATA FRAME
participants = []
for row in challengers['entries']:
    participants_row = {}
    participants_row['summonerId'] = row['summonerId']
    participants_row['summonerName'] = row['summonerName']
    participants_row['leaguePoints'] = row['leaguePoints']
    participants_row['wins'] = row['wins']
    participants_row['losses'] = row['losses']
    participants.append(participants_row)
playerTable = pd.DataFrame(participants)
playerTable['rank'] = 'Challenger'
playerTable

In [7]:
playerIds = []
nameURL = "https://na1.api.riotgames.com/lol/summoner/v4/summoners/by-name/"
for i in morePlayers['summonerName']:
    PARAMS = {'region':'na1'} 
    finalURL = nameURL + str(i.replace(" ","%20")) + "?api_key="+api_key
    r = requests.get(url = finalURL, params = PARAMS) 
    makePlayerTable = json.loads(json.dumps(r.json()))
    playerIds.append(makePlayerTable)
    time.sleep(1)

#GET ACCOUNT MATCH HISTORY - FETCH MATCH IDS
time.sleep(121)
counter = 0
accountmatchurl = "https://na1.api.riotgames.com/lol/match/v4/matchlists/by-account/"
matches = []
for i in morePlayers['accountId']:
    PARAMS = {'region':'na1'} 
    finalURL = accountmatchurl + str(i) + "?api_key="+api_key
    r = requests.get(url = finalURL, params = PARAMS) 
    jsondump = json.loads(json.dumps(r.json()))
    matches.append(jsondump)
    counter += 1
    if counter == 100:
        time.sleep(121)
        counter = 0
#matches

#FETCH MATCH ITSELF
time.sleep(121)
matchHistoryURL = 'https://na1.api.riotgames.com/lol/match/v4/matches/'
realMatchInfo = []
counter = 0
for i in actualMatches[0:1000]:
    PARAMS = {'region':'na1', 'queue':'RANKED_SOLO_5x5'} 
    finalURL = matchHistoryURL + str(i) + "?api_key=" + api_key
    r = requests.get(url = finalURL, params = PARAMS) 
    jsondump = json.loads(json.dumps(r.json()))
    #print(str(jsondump) + "\n\n\n")
    try:
        if jsondump["gameMode"] == "CLASSIC":
            realMatchInfo.append(jsondump)
    except KeyError:
        pass #accessed too many
    #time.sleep(1)
    counter = counter + 1
    if counter == 100:
        counter = 0
        time.sleep(121)

#WRANGLE ACTUAL GAME INFORMATION TO PUT INTO DF
try:
    matchHistorydf = pd.DataFrame()
    tcount = 0
    for match in realMatchInfo[0:1000]:
        matchInfo = []
        matchDict = {}
        #print(match['gameId'])
        matchDict['gameId'] = match['gameId']

        for winner in match['teams']:
            #matchDict['teamId'] = winner['teamId']
            matchDict['TeamTwoWin'] = winner['win']
            #winOrder = []
            #winOrder.append(winner['win'])
        #matchDict['win'] = winOrder#[winOrder['win'] for winOrder in winner]
        champList = []
        roleList = []
        for champ in match['participants']:
            champList.append(champ['championId'])
            if champ['timeline']['lane'] == "BOTTOM":
                roleList.append(champ['timeline']['role'])
            else:
                roleList.append(champ['timeline']['lane'])
            #champ['timeline']['role'] #for adc/supp
            #roleList.append(champ['stats']['timeline']['lane'])
            #print("Champions: " + str(champ['championId']))
        #matchDict['Team1ChampionIds'] = champList[0:5]
        #matchDict['Team2ChampionIds'] = champList[5:]

        matchDict['Team1P1'] = champList[0]
        matchDict['Team1P2'] = champList[1]
        matchDict['Team1P3'] = champList[2]
        matchDict['Team1P4'] = champList[3]
        matchDict['Team1P5'] = champList[4]

        matchDict['Team2P1'] = champList[5]
        matchDict['Team2P2'] = champList[6]
        matchDict['Team2P3'] = champList[7]
        matchDict['Team2P4'] = champList[8]
        matchDict['Team2P5'] = champList[9]
        
        
        
        matchDict['Team1P1Role'] = roleList[0]
        matchDict['Team1P2Role'] = roleList[1]
        matchDict['Team1P3Role'] = roleList[2]
        matchDict['Team1P4Role'] = roleList[3]
        matchDict['Team1P5Role'] = roleList[4]

        matchDict['Team2P1Role'] = roleList[5]
        matchDict['Team2P2Role'] = roleList[6]
        matchDict['Team2P3Role'] = roleList[7]
        matchDict['Team2P4Role'] = roleList[8]
        matchDict['Team2P5Role'] = roleList[9]

        
        accId, summId = [],[]
        for player in match['participantIdentities']:

            accId.append(player['player']['accountId'])
            summId.append(player['player']['summonerId'])
        #matchDict['Team1accountId'] = accId[0:5]
        #matchDict['Team2accountId'] = accId[5:]
        #matchDict['Team1summonerId'] = summId[0:5]
        #matchDict['Team2summonerId'] = summId[5:]


        matchDict['Team1P1SID'] = summId[0]
        matchDict['Team1P2SID'] = summId[1]
        matchDict['Team1P3SID'] = summId[2]
        matchDict['Team1P4SID'] = summId[3]
        matchDict['Team1P5SID'] = summId[4]

        matchDict['Team2P1SID'] = summId[5]
        matchDict['Team2P2SID'] = summId[6]
        matchDict['Team2P3SID'] = summId[7]
        matchDict['Team2P4SID'] = summId[8]
        matchDict['Team2P5SID'] = summId[9]



        '''
        matchDict['participants'] = players
            matchDict['championId'] = player['championId']
        playerChamps.append(eachChamp)
        '''
        matchInfo.append(matchDict)
        matchHistorydf = pd.concat([matchHistorydf, pd.DataFrame.from_dict(matchInfo)])
        tcount = tcount + 1
    matchHistorydf.drop_duplicates(subset = "gameId", keep = False, inplace = True)
    matchHistorydf.reset_index(drop=True, inplace=True)
    matchHistorydf
except KeyError:
    pass

In [33]:
#GET CHAMPION MASTERIES 
time.sleep(121)
champMasteryUrl = 'https://na1.api.riotgames.com/lol/champion-mastery/v4/champion-masteries/by-summoner/'
counter = 0
masteries = []
for i in morePlayers['summonerId']:
    PARAMS = {'region':'na1'} 
    finalURL = champMasteryUrl + str(i) + "?api_key="+api_key
    r = requests.get(url = finalURL, params = PARAMS) 
    jsondump = json.loads(json.dumps(r.json()))
    masteries.append(jsondump)
    counter = counter + 1
    #time.sleep(1)
    if counter == 100:
        time.sleep(121)
        counter = 0
In [34]:
#PUT JSON INTO TABLE    
playerChampMasteryTable = pd.DataFrame()
counter = 0
try:
    for player in masteries:
        playerChamps = []
        for champ in player:
            #print(player)
            eachChamp = {}
            #print(champ['summonerId'])
            eachChamp['summonerId'] = champ['summonerId']
            eachChamp['championId'] = champ['championId']
            eachChamp['championPoints'] = champ['championPoints']
            playerChamps.append(eachChamp)
        playerChampMasteryTable = pd.concat([playerChampMasteryTable, pd.DataFrame.from_dict(playerChamps)])
        counter += 1
    
except TypeError:
    print(counter)
